OCF_changes_in_parliamentary_history_list_dates_add = {
	log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Mission OCF_changes_in_parliamentary_history_list_dates_add"
	#历史折线图的时间存储器 玩家桑~泥也不希望折线图看不到时间罢
	add_to_array = {
		global.OCF_changes_in_parliamentary_history_list_dates = global.date
		index = 0
	}
}

#宣战
OCF_After_collapse_government_Declare_war = {
	every_other_country = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = OCF_After_collapse_government_countries_flag
		}
		IF = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_war_with = ROOT
				}
			}
			declare_war_on = {
				target = PREV
				type = annex_everything
			}
		}
	}
	every_state = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				is_core_of = EIA
				is_core_of = INP
				is_core_of = OFC
				is_core_of = KEZ
				is_core_of = SIE
				is_core_of = FLA
				is_core_of = KCL
				is_core_of = KGF
				is_core_of = ROM
				is_core_of = TKD
				is_core_of = GFZ
				is_core_of = BRI
			}
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = OCF_After_collapse_government_countries_flag
			}
			add_state_core = PREV
		}
	}
}

#内战结束
OCF_end_of_civil_war = {
	OCF = {
		remove_from_array = {
			global.has_ruling_coalition = THIS
		}
		OCF_eliminate_current_ruling_party = yes
		OCF_clear_all_deputy_leaders = yes
		set_country_flag = OCF_abolition_parliament_yes_flag
		transfer_state = 115
		add_state_core = 115
		inherit_technology = ROOT
		set_variable = {
			OCF_bill = 150
		}
		country_event = {
			id = OCF.2
			days = 4			#回收海雾舰队
		}
		load_focus_tree = NO_focus_tree		#载入空国策，以后判断载入什么
	}
	ROOT = {
		#转移所有海军 会有海军吗？
		transfer_navy = {
			target = OCF
		}
	}
	every_country = {
		#吞并其余势力
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = OCF_After_collapse_government_countries_flag
			NOT = {
				tag = ROOT
			}
		}
		ROOT = {
			annex_country = {
				target = PREV
				transfer_troops = yes
			}
		}
		every_unit_leader = {
			set_nationality = OCF
		}
	}
	ROOT = {
		#吞并所有将领
		every_unit_leader = {
			set_nationality = OCF
		}
	}
	if = {
		#一下就是各种检测战胜国，这注释我就不写了
		limit = {
			tag = INP
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_character = INP_Eblana_Dublinn
			}
			set_nationality = {
				target_country = OCF
				character = INP_Eblana_Dublinn
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_character = INP_Reed_The_Flame_Shadow
			}
			set_nationality = {
				target_country = OCF
				character = INP_Reed_The_Flame_Shadow
			}
		}
		OCF = {
			set_cosmetic_tag = INP_unification
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = fascism
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = fascism
				popularity = 1
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = fascism
				long_name = INP_fascism_party_2_long
				name = INP_fascism_party_2
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = democratic
				long_name = INP_democratic_party_2_long
				name = INP_democratic_party_2
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = communism
				long_name = INP_communism_party_long
				name = INP_communism_party
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = neutrality
				long_name = INP_neutrality_party_long
				name = INP_neutrality_party
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = reactionism
				long_name = INP_reactionism_party_long
				name = INP_reactionism_party
			}
			promote_character = {
				character = INP_Eblana_Dublinn
				ideology = sub_Regressivism
			}
			promote_character = {
				character = INP_Eblana_Dublinn
				ideology = sub_Facism
			}
			add_ideas = INP_idea_Reed_The_Flame_Shadow
			annex_country = {
				target = ROOT
				transfer_troops = yes
			}
			change_tag_from = ROOT
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				tag = OFC
				tag = KEZ
				tag = SIE
				tag = KCL
				tag = KGF
				tag = BRI
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				TAG = KEZ
			}
			set_global_flag = OCF_civil_war_so_it_was_unified_flag_KEZ
		}
		OCF = {
			set_cosmetic_tag = OCF_fourth
			annex_country = {
				target = ROOT
				transfer_troops = yes
			}
			change_tag_from = ROOT
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			tag = TKD
		}
		OCF = {
			set_cosmetic_tag = TKD_kingdom
			annex_country = {
				target = ROOT
				transfer_troops = yes
			}
			change_tag_from = ROOT
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			tag = GFZ
		}
		OCF = {
			set_cosmetic_tag = GFZ_unification
			annex_country = {
				target = ROOT
				transfer_troops = yes
			}
			change_tag_from = ROOT
		}
	}
	every_state = {
		limit = {
			has_state_flag = regions_belonging_OCF_flag
		}
		remove_core_of = ANA
		remove_core_of = OFC
		remove_core_of = KEZ
		remove_core_of = SIE
		remove_core_of = FLA
		remove_core_of = KCL
		remove_core_of = KGF
		remove_core_of = ROM
		remove_core_of = TKD
		remove_core_of = GFZ
		remove_core_of = BRI
		remove_core_of = INP
		remove_core_of = EIA
		add_core_of = OCF
		transfer_state_to = OCF
	}
}

OCF_brgnews_6_scripted_effects = {
	log = "[GetDateText]: ROOT: [Root.GetName] OCF_brgnews_6_scripted_effects"

	clr_global_flag = BRG_2_a_flag
	# log = "[GetDateText]: FROM: [From.GetName] ROOT: [Root.GetName] on_capitulation"

	# set_global_flag = show_peace_popup_alert
	# set_global_flag = war_won
	# FROM = {
	# 	save_global_event_target_as = winning_country
	# }
	# ROOT = {
	# 	save_global_event_target_as = losing_country
	# }
	# IRIS_peace_popup_determine_allies = yes
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				is_ally_with = OCF
				original_tag = OCF
			}
			has_war_with = USF
		}
		if = {

			}

				# USF = {

				# }

				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_ally_with = OCF

					}
					has_war_with = USF

					# 	has_country_flag = BRG_civil_war_General_Douglas_MacArthur_flag
					# }

					white_peace = USF
				}
			}
		}
		else = {

				every_country = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							is_ally_with = OCF
							original_tag = OCF
						}
						has_war_with = USF
					}
					THIS = {
						white_peace = USF
					}

			}
		}
	}
	else = {

					}
					has_war_with = OCF
				}

					white_peace = OCF
				}
			}
		}

#崩溃的政府体系计算
OCF_collapsed_government_system_yes = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = OCF_collapsed_government_system
		}
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = OCF_collapsed_government_system
			add_idea = OCF_collapsed_government_system_1
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = OCF_collapsed_government_system_1
		}
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = OCF_collapsed_government_system_1
			add_idea = OCF_collapsed_government_system_2
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = OCF_collapsed_government_system_2
		}
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = OCF_collapsed_government_system_2
			add_idea = OCF_collapsed_government_system_3
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = OCF_collapsed_government_system_3
		}
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = OCF_collapsed_government_system_3
			add_idea = OCF_collapsed_government_system_4
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = OCF_collapsed_government_system_4
		}
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = OCF_collapsed_government_system_4
			add_idea = OCF_collapsed_government_system_5
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = OCF_collapsed_government_system_5
		}
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = OCF_collapsed_government_system_5
			add_idea = OCF_collapsed_government_system_6
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = OCF_collapsed_government_system_6
		}
		remove_ideas = OCF_collapsed_government_system_6
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = {
				has_idea = OCF_collapsed_government_system_7
			}
		}
		add_ideas = OCF_collapsed_government_system_7
	}
}

OCF_Random_infrastructure = {
	#随机给个基建
	random_owned_controlled_state = {
		limit = {
			free_building_slots = {
				building = infrastructure
				size > 0
			}
			OR = {
				is_in_home_area = yes
				NOT = {
					owner = {
						any_owned_state = {
							free_building_slots = {
								building = infrastructure
								size > 0
							}
							is_in_home_area = yes
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		add_building_construction = {
			type = infrastructure
			level = 1
			instant_build = yes
		}
		add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
	}
}

#军工
OCF_Randomly_give_military_industry = {
	random_owned_controlled_state = {
		limit = {
			free_building_slots = {
				building = arms_factory
				size > 0
				include_locked = yes
			}
			OR = {
				is_in_home_area = yes
				NOT = {
					owner = {
						any_owned_state = {
							free_building_slots = {
								building = arms_factory
								size > 0
								include_locked = yes
							}
							is_in_home_area = yes
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
		add_building_construction = {
			type = arms_factory
			level = 1
			instant_build = yes
		}
	}
}

#设置加成
OCF_federal_film_company_bonus = {
	set_variable = {
		OCF_federal_film_company_stability_factor = 0
	}
	#稳定
	set_variable = {
		OCF_federal_film_company_industrial_capacity_factory = 0
	}
	#产出
	set_variable = {
		OCF_federal_film_company_industrial_capacity_dockyard = 0
	}
	#船坞
	set_variable = {
		OCF_federal_film_company_research_speed_factor = 0
	}
	#科研
	set_variable = {
		OCF_federal_film_company_production_speed_buildings_factor = 0
	}
	#建造
	set_variable = {
		OCF_federal_film_company_army_attack_factor = 0
	}
	#攻击
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				OCF_poster_iconType_variable_1 = 2
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			OCF_federal_film_company_production_speed_buildings_factor = 0.07
		}
	}
	#幸运星
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				OCF_poster_iconType_variable_1 = 3
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			OCF_federal_film_company_research_speed_factor = 0.05
		}
		set_variable = {
			OCF_federal_film_company_industrial_capacity_factory = 0.03
		}
	}
	#石之门
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				OCF_poster_iconType_variable_1 = 6
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			OCF_federal_film_company_stability_factor = 0.1
		}
	}
	#猫咪日常
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				OCF_poster_iconType_variable_1 = 7
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			OCF_federal_film_company_research_speed_factor = 0.12
		}
		set_variable = {
			OCF_federal_film_company_stability_factor = -0.08
		}
	}
	#快要坏掉的八音盒
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				OCF_poster_iconType_variable_1 = 8
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			OCF_federal_film_company_industrial_capacity_dockyard = 0.1
		}
	}
	#苍蓝钢铁
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				OCF_poster_iconType_variable_1 = 9
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			OCF_federal_film_company_research_speed_factor = 0.08
		}
	}
	#笨拙至极的上野
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				OCF_poster_iconType_variable_1 = 10
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			OCF_federal_film_company_army_attack_factor = 0.07
		}
	}
	#爱杀宝贝
}

OCF_initialize_workshop = {
	set_variable = {
		OCF.current_level_of_weapon_reliability_optimization = OCF.weapon_reliability
	}
	#武器可靠性优化程度
	set_variable = {
		OCF.current_level_of_weapon_availability_optimization = OCF.weapon_kill
	}
	#武器可用性优化程度
	set_variable = {
		OCF.optimization_degree_of_weapon_structure = OCF.weapon_structure
	}
	#当前武器结构性优化程度
	clr_country_flag = OCF_entrusting_grand_chancellor_flag	#去除大执政官标记
}

#每周工坊数值增加
OCF_workshop_values_increase = {
	set_variable = {
		OCF.weapon_reliability_increase = OCF.weapon_reliability_increase_add
	}
	add_to_variable = {
		OCF.weapon_reliability_increase = modifier@ocf_weapon_reliability_correct
	}
	set_variable = {
		OCF.weapon_kill_increase = OCF.weapon_kill_increase_add
	}
	add_to_variable = {
		OCF.weapon_kill_increase = modifier@ocf_weapon_kill_correct
	}
	set_variable = {
		OCF.weapon_structure_increase = OCF.weapon_structure_increase_add
	}
	add_to_variable = {
		OCF.weapon_structure_increase = modifier@ocf_weapon_structure_correct
	}
	add_to_variable = {
		OCF.weapon_reliability_progress = OCF.weapon_reliability_increase
	}
	#武器可靠性
	add_to_variable = {
		OCF.weapon_kill_progress = OCF.weapon_kill_increase
	}
	#武器杀伤
	add_to_variable = {
		OCF.weapon_structure_progress = OCF.weapon_structure_increase
	}
	#武器结构
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				OCF.weapon_reliability_progress > 100
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			OCF.weapon_reliability = 1
		}
		#可靠
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					OCF.weapon_reliability > 100
				}
			}
			set_variable = {
				OCF.weapon_reliability = 100
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			OCF.weapon_reliability_progress = 0
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				OCF.weapon_kill_progress > 100
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			OCF.weapon_kill = 1
		}
		#杀伤
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					OCF.weapon_kill > 100
				}
			}
			set_variable = {
				OCF.weapon_kill = 100
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			OCF.weapon_kill_progress = 0
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				OCF.weapon_structure_progress > 100
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			OCF.weapon_structure = 1
		}
		#结构
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					OCF.weapon_structure > 100
				}
			}
			set_variable = {
				OCF.weapon_structure = 100
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			OCF.weapon_structure_progress = 0
		}
	}
}

#防止工坊数值溢出
OCF_prevent_overflow_of_workshop_values = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				OCF.current_level_of_weapon_reliability_optimization > 100
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			OCF.current_level_of_weapon_reliability_optimization = 100
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				OCF.current_level_of_weapon_availability_optimization > 100
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			OCF.current_level_of_weapon_availability_optimization = 100
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				OCF.optimization_degree_of_weapon_structure > 100
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			OCF.optimization_degree_of_weapon_structure = 100
		}
	}
}

#判定工坊结果
OCF_judging_workshop_results = {
	set_variable = {
		OCF.weapon_result = OCF.current_level_of_weapon_reliability_optimization
	}
	#先算一下平均值
	add_to_variable = {
		OCF.weapon_result = OCF.current_level_of_weapon_availability_optimization
	}
	add_to_variable = {
		OCF.weapon_result = OCF.optimization_degree_of_weapon_structure
	}
	divide_variable = {
		OCF.weapon_result = 3
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			is_ai = yes
		}
		OCF_judging_workshop_results_5 = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				OCF.weapon_result>99
			}
			is_ai = no
		}
		OCF_judging_workshop_results_10 = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				OCF.weapon_result>89
			}
			is_ai = no
		}
		OCF_judging_workshop_results_9 = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				OCF.weapon_result>79
			}
			is_ai = no
		}
		OCF_judging_workshop_results_8 = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				OCF.weapon_result>69
			}
			is_ai = no
		}
		OCF_judging_workshop_results_7 = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				OCF.weapon_result>59
			}
			is_ai = no
		}
		OCF_judging_workshop_results_6 = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				OCF.weapon_result>49
			}
			is_ai = no
		}
		OCF_judging_workshop_results_5 = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				OCF.weapon_result>39
			}
			is_ai = no
		}
		OCF_judging_workshop_results_4 = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				OCF.weapon_result>29
			}
			is_ai = no
		}
		OCF_judging_workshop_results_3 = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				OCF.weapon_result>19
			}
			is_ai = no
		}
		OCF_judging_workshop_results_2 = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				OCF.weapon_result>9
			}
			is_ai = no
		}
		OCF_judging_workshop_results_1 = yes
	}
	else = {
		OCF_judging_workshop_results_0 = yes
	}
}

#武器产生列表
OCF_judging_workshop_results_0 = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				OCF.attack_defense_manufacturing_weapon_number = 1
			}
		}
		set_technology = {
			ocf_refined_magic_stone_tech = 1
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				OCF.attack_defense_manufacturing_weapon_number = 2
			}
		}
		set_technology = {
			ocf_refined_magic_stone_2_tech = 1
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				OCF.attack_defense_manufacturing_weapon_number = 3
			}
		}
		set_technology = {
			ocf_magic_stone_modified_household_broom_tech = 1
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				OCF.attack_defense_manufacturing_weapon_number = 4
			}
		}
		set_technology = {
			ocf_small_magic_wand_tech = 1
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				OCF.attack_defense_manufacturing_weapon_number = 5
			}
		}
		set_technology = {
			ocf_small_magic_wand_2_tech = 1
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {

			}
		}
		set_technology = {

OCF_artificial_intelligence_flashing_in = {
	115 = {
		create_unit = {
			division = "division_template = \"Test\" start_experience_factor = 1 start_equipment_factor = 1.0"
			owner = PREV
			count = 8
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = OCF_strengthening_AI_flag }
			create_unit = {
				division = "division_template = \"Test\" start_experience_factor = 1 start_equipment_factor = 1.0"
				owner = PREV
				count = 20
			}
		}
	}
}

#科技修正添加
#扩编工程兵团
enable_ocf_expanded_engineer_corps = {
	custom_override_tooltip = {
		tooltip = {
			localization_key = IRIS_tooltip_enable_hidden_tech
			TECH = country_culture|ocf_expanded_engineer_corps
			EFFECT = tech_effect|ocf_expanded_engineer_corps
		}
		set_technology = {
			ocf_expanded_engineer_corps = 1
			popup = no
		}
	}
}

#扩编海军陆战队
enable_ocf_expand_marine_corps = {
	custom_override_tooltip = {
		tooltip = {
			localization_key = IRIS_tooltip_enable_hidden_tech
			TECH = country_culture|ocf_expand_marine_corps
			EFFECT = tech_effect|ocf_expand_marine_corps
		}
		set_technology = {
			ocf_expand_marine_corps = 1
			popup = no
		}
	}
}

			EFFECT = tech_effect|ocf_improved_logistics
		}
		set_technology = {
			ocf_improved_logistics = 1
			popup = no
		}
	}
}

#添加资金
OCF_spending_funds_other = {
	custom_effect_tooltip = OCF_spending_funds_change
	custom_effect_tooltip = {
		localization_key = OCF_SPENDING_FUNDS_TT
		FUNDS = "[?temp_bill]"
	}
	add_to_variable = {
		OCF_bill = temp_bill
	}
}

#添加资金
OCF_spending_funds_temp = {
	custom_effect_tooltip = {
		localization_key = OCF_SPENDING_FUNDS_TT
		FUNDS = "[?temp_fund_exchange_button]"
	}
	add_to_variable = {
		OCF_fund_exchange_buttonType_var = temp_fund_exchange_button
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				OCF_fund_exchange_buttonType_var < 0
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			OCF_fund_exchange_buttonType_var = 0
		}
	}

	#关闭动画
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { OCF_fund_exchange_buttonType_var = 0 }
			NOT = { check_variable = { OCF_bank_bill_y = 140 } }
		}
		add_to_variable = { OCF_bank_bill_animation = 1 }
		modulo_variable = { OCF_bank_bill_animation = 2 }
		set_variable = { OCF_bank_bill_frame = 501501 }
		set_variable = { OCF_bank_bill_y = 40 }
	}

	#打开动画
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { OCF_fund_exchange_buttonType_var > 0 }
			NOT = { check_variable = { OCF_bank_bill_y = 240 } }
		}
		add_to_variable = { OCF_bank_bill_animation = 1 }
		modulo_variable = { OCF_bank_bill_animation = 2 }
		set_variable = { OCF_bank_bill_frame = 1500500 }
		set_variable = { OCF_bank_bill_y = 240 }
	}
}

#初始化资金调整
set_custom_slider = {
	for_loop_effect = {
		start = 0
		end = 101
		value = val
		add_to_array = {
			slider_buttons = val
		}
	}
	for_loop_effect = {
		start = 0
		end = 101
		value = val
		add_to_array = {
			OCF_adjusting_military_spending_buttons = val
		}
	}
	for_loop_effect = {
		start = 0
		end = 101
		value = val
		add_to_array = {
			OCF_adjusting_education_expenses_buttons = val
		}
	}
	for_loop_effect = {
		start = 0
		end = 101
		value = val
		add_to_array = {
			OCF_adjusting_medical_treatment_buttons = val
		}
	}
}

##资金获取（效果预估）
OCF_obtain_banknotes_effect_estimation = {
	set_variable = {
		tax_impact_effect_estimation = current_int
	}
	multiply_variable = {
		tax_impact_effect_estimation = -0.1
	}
	#计算修正（抬高税收稳定度修正）
	set_variable = {
		ocf_tax_revenue_stability_correction_2 = 1
	}
	add_to_variable = {
		ocf_tax_revenue_stability_correction_2 = modifier@ocf_tax_revenue_stability_correction
	}
	multiply_variable = {
		tax_impact_effect_estimation = ocf_tax_revenue_stability_correction_2
	}
	multiply_variable = {
		tax_impact_effect_estimation = 0.004
	}
	add_to_variable = { tax_impact_effect_estimation = 0.005 }
	log = "[?tax_impact_effect_estimation]"
	#获取民用工厂
	set_variable = {
		OCF_obtain_banknotes_variable = ROOT.num_of_civilian_factories
	}
	#计算修正（民用工厂税收贡献修正）
	set_variable = {
		ocf_tax_revenue_civil_factories_correction_2 = 1
	}
	add_to_variable = {
		ocf_tax_revenue_civil_factories_correction_2 = modifier@ocf_tax_revenue_civil_factories_correction
	}
	multiply_variable = {
		OCF_obtain_banknotes_variable = ocf_tax_revenue_civil_factories_correction_2
	}
	#获取稳定度
	set_variable = {
		OCF_stability_variable_30 = ROOT.stability
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				OCF_stability_variable_30 < 0.3
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			OCF_stability_variable_30 = 0.3
		}
	}
	multiply_variable = {
		OCF_obtain_banknotes_variable = OCF_stability_variable_30
	}
	#税收基础值
	set_variable = {
		OCF_obtain_banknotes_variable_markup = 1
	}
	set_variable = {
		tax_impact = current_int
	}
	multiply_variable = {
		tax_impact = 0.1
	}
	add_to_variable = {
		OCF_obtain_banknotes_variable_markup = tax_impact
	}
	multiply_variable = {
		OCF_obtain_banknotes_variable = OCF_obtain_banknotes_variable_markup
	}
	#计算修正（税收修正）
	set_variable = {
		ocf_tax_revenue_correction_2 = 1
	}
	add_to_variable = {
		ocf_tax_revenue_correction_2 = modifier@ocf_tax_revenue_correction
	}
	multiply_variable = {
		OCF_obtain_banknotes_variable = ocf_tax_revenue_correction_2
	}
	OCF_obtain_banknotes_threshold_estimate = yes
	set_variable = {
		OCF_spending_funds_variable = 2
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_war = yes
		}
		set_variable = {
			OCF_spending_funds_variable_has_war = 2.5
		}
		subtract_from_variable = {
			OCF_spending_funds_variable_has_war = ROOT.has_war_support
		}
		#获取战争支持
		set_variable = {
			OCF_number_military_personnel = ROOT.deployed_army_manpower_k
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			OCF_number_military_personnel = ROOT.deployed_navy_manpower_k
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			OCF_number_military_personnel = ROOT.deployed_airforce_manpower_k
		}
		divide_variable = {
			OCF_number_military_personnel = 500
		}
		#军队花费
		add_to_variable = {
			OCF_number_military_personnel = 1
		}
		multiply_variable = {
			OCF_spending_funds_variable = OCF_spending_funds_variable_has_war
		}
		multiply_variable = {
			OCF_spending_funds_variable = OCF_number_military_personnel
		}
		#计算修正（军费开支修正）
		set_variable = {
			ocf_capital_military_expenses_correction_2 = 1
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			ocf_capital_military_expenses_correction_2 = modifier@ocf_capital_military_expenses_correction
		}
		multiply_variable = {
			OCF_spending_funds_variable = ocf_capital_military_expenses_correction_2
		}
		#计算修正（军费战时开支修正）
		set_variable = {
			ocf_capital_military_expenses_war_correction_2 = 1
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			ocf_capital_military_expenses_war_correction_2 = modifier@ocf_capital_military_expenses_war_correction
		}
		multiply_variable = {
			OCF_spending_funds_variable = ocf_capital_military_expenses_war_correction_2
		}
		#减去军队花费
	}
	else = {
		set_variable = {
			OCF_spending_funds_variable_has_war = 2.5
		}
		subtract_from_variable = {
			OCF_spending_funds_variable_has_war = ROOT.has_war_support
		}
		#获取战争支持
		set_variable = {
			OCF_number_military_personnel = ROOT.deployed_army_manpower_k
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			OCF_number_military_personnel = ROOT.deployed_navy_manpower_k
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			OCF_number_military_personnel = ROOT.deployed_airforce_manpower_k
		}
		divide_variable = {
			OCF_number_military_personnel = 1200
		}
		#军队花费
		add_to_variable = {
			OCF_number_military_personnel = 1
		}
		multiply_variable = {
			OCF_spending_funds_variable = OCF_spending_funds_variable_has_war
		}
		multiply_variable = {
			OCF_spending_funds_variable = OCF_number_military_personnel
		}
		#计算修正（军费开支修正）
		set_variable = {
			ocf_capital_military_expenses_correction_2 = 1
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			ocf_capital_military_expenses_correction_2 = modifier@ocf_capital_military_expenses_correction
		}
		multiply_variable = {
			OCF_spending_funds_variable = ocf_capital_military_expenses_correction_2
		}
		#计算修正（军费维护开支修正）
		set_variable = {
			ocf_capital_military_expenses_no_war_correction_2 = 1
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			ocf_capital_military_expenses_no_war_correction_2 = modifier@ocf_capital_military_expenses_no_war_correction
		}
		multiply_variable = {
			OCF_spending_funds_variable = ocf_capital_military_expenses_no_war_correction_2
		}
		#减去军队花费
	}
	#军费修正
	set_variable = {
		OCF_obtain_banknotes_variable_markup = 0
	}
	add_to_variable = {
		OCF_obtain_banknotes_variable_markup = adjusting_military_spending_int
	}
	set_variable = {
		military_expenditure_impact_effect_estimation = adjusting_military_spending_int
	}
	add_to_variable = {
		military_expenditure_impact_effect_estimation = -20
	}
	#默认值
	multiply_variable = {
		military_expenditure_impact_effect_estimation = 0.2
	}
	#加成数值
	multiply_variable = {
		military_expenditure_impact_effect_estimation = 0.025
	}
	#教育修正
	set_variable = {
		adjusting_education_expenses_int_2 = adjusting_education_expenses_int
	}
	#计算修正（教育开支修正）
	set_variable = {
		ocf_capital_educate_expenses_correction_2 = 1
	}
	add_to_variable = {
		ocf_capital_educate_expenses_correction_2 = modifier@ocf_capital_educate_expenses_correction
	}
	multiply_variable = {
		adjusting_education_expenses_int_2 = ocf_capital_educate_expenses_correction_2
	}
	add_to_variable = {
		OCF_obtain_banknotes_variable_markup = adjusting_education_expenses_int_2
	}
	set_variable = {
		education_revision_effect_estimation = adjusting_education_expenses_int
	}
	multiply_variable = {
		education_revision_effect_estimation = 0.2
	}
	add_to_variable = {
		education_revision_effect_estimation = 0
	}
	#加成数值
	multiply_variable = {
		education_revision_effect_estimation = 0.02
	}
	#医疗修正
	set_variable = {
		adjusting_medical_treatment_int_2 = adjusting_medical_treatment_int
	}
	#计算修正（医疗开支修正）
	set_variable = {
		ocf_capital_medical_expenses_correction_2 = 1
	}
	add_to_variable = {
		ocf_capital_medical_expenses_correction_2 = modifier@ocf_capital_medical_expenses_correction
	}
	multiply_variable = {
		adjusting_education_expenses_int_2 = ocf_capital_medical_expenses_correction_2
	}
	add_to_variable = {
		OCF_obtain_banknotes_variable_markup = adjusting_medical_treatment_int_2
	}
	set_variable = {
		medical_correction_effect_estimation = adjusting_medical_treatment_int
	}
	add_to_variable = {
		medical_correction_effect_estimation = -7.5
	}
	#默认值
	multiply_variable = {
		medical_correction_effect_estimation = 0.2
	}
	#加成数值
	multiply_variable = {
		medical_correction_effect_estimation = 0.05
	}
	#加成数值
	multiply_variable = {
		OCF_obtain_banknotes_variable_markup = 0.1
	}
	add_to_variable = {
		OCF_obtain_banknotes_variable_markup = 1
	}
	#默认值
	multiply_variable = {
		OCF_spending_funds_variable = OCF_obtain_banknotes_variable_markup
	}
	#计算修正（资金总开支修正）
	set_variable = {
		ocf_capital_expenditure_correction_2 = 1
	}
	add_to_variable = {
		ocf_capital_expenditure_correction_2 = modifier@ocf_capital_expenditure_correction
	}
	multiply_variable = {
		OCF_spending_funds_variable = ocf_capital_expenditure_correction_2
	}
}

#资金（ 获取资金）
OCF_obtain_banknotes = {
	#获取民用工厂
	set_variable = {
		OCF_obtain_banknotes_variable = ROOT.num_of_civilian_factories
	}
	#计算修正（民用工厂税收贡献修正）
	set_variable = {
		ocf_tax_revenue_civil_factories_correction_2 = 1
	}
	add_to_variable = {
		ocf_tax_revenue_civil_factories_correction_2 = modifier@ocf_tax_revenue_civil_factories_correction
	}
	multiply_variable = {
		OCF_obtain_banknotes_variable = ocf_tax_revenue_civil_factories_correction_2
	}
	#获取稳定度
	set_variable = {
		OCF_stability_variable_30 = ROOT.stability
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				OCF_stability_variable_30 < 0.3
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			OCF_stability_variable_30 = 0.3
		}
	}
	multiply_variable = {
		OCF_obtain_banknotes_variable = OCF_stability_variable_30
	}
	#税收基础值
	set_variable = {
		OCF_obtain_banknotes_variable_markup = 1
	}
	set_variable = {
		tax_impact = current_int
	}
	multiply_variable = {
		tax_impact = 0.1
	}
	add_to_variable = {
		OCF_obtain_banknotes_variable_markup = tax_impact
	}
	multiply_variable = {
		OCF_obtain_banknotes_variable = OCF_obtain_banknotes_variable_markup
	}
	#计算修正（税收修正）
	set_variable = {
		ocf_tax_revenue_correction_2 = 1
	}
	add_to_variable = {
		ocf_tax_revenue_correction_2 = modifier@ocf_tax_revenue_correction
	}
	multiply_variable = {
		OCF_obtain_banknotes_variable = ocf_tax_revenue_correction_2
	}
	set_variable = {
		tax_impact = current_int
	}
	#显示的稳定度下降
	add_to_variable = {
		tax_impact = 0
	}
	#废弃
	#默认值
	multiply_variable = {
		tax_impact = -0.1
	}
	#计算修正（抬高税收稳定度修正）
	set_variable = {
		ocf_tax_revenue_stability_correction_2 = 1
	}
	add_to_variable = {
		ocf_tax_revenue_stability_correction_2 = modifier@ocf_tax_revenue_stability_correction
	}
	multiply_variable = {
		tax_impact = ocf_tax_revenue_stability_correction_2
	}
	set_variable = {
		tax_impact_100 = tax_impact
	}
	#加成数值
	multiply_variable = {
		tax_impact_100 = 0.004
	}
	add_to_variable = { tax_impact_100 = 0.005 }
	#加成数值
	OCF_obtain_banknotes_threshold = yes
	add_to_variable = {
		OCF_bill = OCF_obtain_banknotes_variable
	}
	if = {
		#AI的每月额外资金(他都是AI了你就让着他呗 >_<||| )
		limit = {
			is_ai = yes
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			OCF_bill = 30
		}
	}
	OCF_spending_funds = yes
}

#获取资金阈值（预估）
OCF_obtain_banknotes_threshold_estimate = {
	set_variable = {
		OCF_obtain_banknotes_threshold_variable = 200		#这里就是基础值
	}
	#计算修正（税收上限修正）
	add_to_variable = {
		OCF_obtain_banknotes_threshold_variable = modifier@ocf_tax_cap_correction
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				OCF_obtain_banknotes_variable > OCF_obtain_banknotes_threshold_variable
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			OCF_obtain_banknotes_variable = OCF_obtain_banknotes_threshold_variable
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				OCF_obtain_banknotes_variable < 2
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			OCF_obtain_banknotes_variable = 2
		}
	}
}

#获取资金阈值
OCF_obtain_banknotes_threshold = {
	set_variable = {
		OCF_obtain_banknotes_threshold_variable = 200
	}
	#计算修正（税收上限修正）
	add_to_variable = {
		OCF_obtain_banknotes_threshold_variable = modifier@ocf_tax_cap_correction
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				OCF_obtain_banknotes_variable > OCF_obtain_banknotes_threshold_variable
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			OCF_obtain_banknotes_variable = OCF_obtain_banknotes_threshold_variable
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				OCF_obtain_banknotes_variable < 2
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			OCF_obtain_banknotes_variable = 2
		}
	}
	add_to_variable = {
		OCF_bill = modifier@ocf_capital_monthly_additional_funds
	}
}

#花费资金
OCF_spending_funds = {
	set_variable = {
		OCF_spending_funds_variable = 2
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_war = yes
		}
		set_variable = {
			OCF_spending_funds_variable_has_war = 2.5
		}
		subtract_from_variable = {
			OCF_spending_funds_variable_has_war = ROOT.has_war_support

		}

		}

			OCF_number_military_personnel = 500
		}
		#军队花费
		add_to_variable = {
			OCF_number_military_personnel = 1
		}
		multiply_variable = {
			OCF_spending_funds_variable = OCF_spending_funds_variable_has_war
		}
		multiply_variable = {
			OCF_spending_funds_variable = OCF_number_military_personnel
		}
		#计算修正（军费开支修正）

		}
		add_to_variable = {

		}
		multiply_variable = {
			OCF_spending_funds_variable = ocf_capital_military_expenses_correction_2

		}
		add_to_variable = {
			ocf_capital_military_expenses_war_correction_2 = modifier@ocf_capital_military_expenses_war_correction

		}

			OCF_number_military_personnel = ROOT.deployed_airforce_manpower_k
		}
		divide_variable = {
			OCF_number_military_personnel = 1200
		}
		#军队花费
		add_to_variable = {
			OCF_number_military_personnel = 1
		}
		multiply_variable = {
			OCF_spending_funds_variable = OCF_spending_funds_variable_has_war
		}
		multiply_variable = {
			OCF_spending_funds_variable = OCF_number_military_personnel
		}
		#计算修正（军费开支修正）
		set_variable = {
			ocf_capital_military_expenses_correction_2 = 1
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			ocf_capital_military_expenses_correction_2 = modifier@ocf_capital_military_expenses_correction
		}
		multiply_variable = {
			OCF_spending_funds_variable = ocf_capital_military_expenses_correction_2
		}
		#计算修正（军费维护开支修正）
		set_variable = {
			ocf_capital_military_expenses_no_war_correction_2 = 1
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			ocf_capital_military_expenses_no_war_correction_2 = modifier@ocf_capital_military_expenses_no_war_correction
		}
		multiply_variable = {
			OCF_spending_funds_variable = ocf_capital_military_expenses_no_war_correction_2
		}
		#减去军队花费
	}
	#军费修正
	set_variable = {
		OCF_obtain_banknotes_variable_markup = 0
	}
	add_to_variable = {
		OCF_obtain_banknotes_variable_markup = adjusting_military_spending_int
	}
	set_variable = {
		military_expenditure_impact = adjusting_military_spending_int
	}
	add_to_variable = {
		military_expenditure_impact = -20
	}
	#默认值
	multiply_variable = {
		military_expenditure_impact = 0.2
	}
	#加成数值
	set_variable = {
		adjusting_military_spending_int_100 = military_expenditure_impact
	}
	#加成数值
	multiply_variable = {
		adjusting_military_spending_int_100 = 0.025
	}
	#加成数值
	#教育修正
	set_variable = {
		adjusting_education_expenses_int_2 = adjusting_education_expenses_int
	}
	#计算修正（教育开支修正）
	set_variable = {
		ocf_capital_educate_expenses_correction_2 = 1
	}
	add_to_variable = {
		ocf_capital_educate_expenses_correction_2 = modifier@ocf_capital_educate_expenses_correction
	}
	multiply_variable = {
		adjusting_education_expenses_int_2 = ocf_capital_educate_expenses_correction_2
	}
	add_to_variable = {
		OCF_obtain_banknotes_variable_markup = adjusting_education_expenses_int_2
	}
	set_variable = {
		education_revision = adjusting_education_expenses_int
	}
	multiply_variable = {
		education_revision = 0.2
	}
	add_to_variable = {
		education_revision = 0
	}
	#默认值
	set_variable = {
		education_revision_100 = education_revision
	}
	#加成数值
	multiply_variable = {
		education_revision_100 = 0.02
	}
	#加成数值
	#医疗修正
	set_variable = {
		adjusting_medical_treatment_int_2 = adjusting_medical_treatment_int
	}
	#计算修正（医疗开支修正）
	set_variable = {
		ocf_capital_medical_expenses_correction_2 = 1
	}
	add_to_variable = {
		ocf_capital_medical_expenses_correction_2 = modifier@ocf_capital_medical_expenses_correction
	}
	multiply_variable = {
		adjusting_education_expenses_int_2 = ocf_capital_medical_expenses_correction_2
	}
	add_to_variable = {
		OCF_obtain_banknotes_variable_markup = adjusting_medical_treatment_int_2
	}
	set_variable = {
		medical_correction = adjusting_medical_treatment_int
	}
	add_to_variable = {
		medical_correction = -7.5
	}
	#默认值
	multiply_variable = {
		medical_correction = 0.2
	}
	#加成数值
	set_variable = {
		medical_correction_100 = medical_correction
	}
	#加成数值
	multiply_variable = {
		medical_correction_100 = 0.05
	}
	#加成数值
	multiply_variable = {
		OCF_obtain_banknotes_variable_markup = 0.1
	}
	add_to_variable = {
		OCF_obtain_banknotes_variable_markup = 1
	}
	#默认值
	multiply_variable = {
		OCF_spending_funds_variable = OCF_obtain_banknotes_variable_markup
	}
	#计算修正（资金总开支修正）
	set_variable = {
		ocf_capital_expenditure_correction_2 = 1
	}
	add_to_variable = {
		ocf_capital_expenditure_correction_2 = modifier@ocf_capital_expenditure_correction
	}
	multiply_variable = {
		OCF_spending_funds_variable = ocf_capital_expenditure_correction_2
	}
	subtract_from_variable = {
		OCF_bill = OCF_spending_funds_variable
	}
	#每月花费
}

#检测每月收入
OCF_check_monthly_income = {
	set_temp_variable = {
		OCF_check_monthly_income_temp = OCF_obtain_banknotes_variable
	}
	add_to_temp_variable = {
		OCF_check_monthly_income_temp = modifier@ocf_capital_monthly_additional_funds
	}
	subtract_from_temp_variable = {
		OCF_check_monthly_income_temp = OCF_spending_funds_variable
	}
	set_temp_variable = {
		alert_id = token:alert_OCF_Income_deficit
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				OCF_check_monthly_income_temp < 0
			}
		}
		add_IRIS_alert_unless_exists = yes
	}
	else = {
		del_IRIS_alert = yes
	}
	log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Mission OCF_check_monthly_income 检测每月收入：[?OCF_check_monthly_income_temp]"
}

OCF_NOW_number_faction_interactions = {
	custom_effect_tooltip = OCF_del_NOW_number_faction_interactions_var_tt
	add_to_variable = {
		NOW_number_faction_interactions_var = NOW_number_faction_interactions_temp
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				NOW_number_faction_interactions_var > MAX_number_faction_interactions_var
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			NOW_number_faction_interactions_var = MAX_number_faction_interactions_var
		}
	}
}

#添加可通过议案
OCF_proposal_can_passed_add = {
	add_to_variable = {
		ROOT.proposal_that_needs_passed = 1
	}
	OCF_proposal_can_passed_add_sign = yes
}

#移除可通过议案
OCF_proposal_can_passed_del = {
	add_to_variable = {
		ROOT.proposal_that_needs_passed = -1
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				ROOT.proposal_that_needs_passed < 0
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			ROOT.proposal_that_needs_passed = 0
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				ROOT.proposal_that_needs_passed < 1
			}
		}
		OCF_proposal_can_passed_del_sign = yes
	}
}

#添加可通过议案-标识
OCF_proposal_can_passed_add_sign = {
	set_temp_variable = {
		alert_id = token:alert_OCF_proposal_passed
	}
	add_IRIS_alert_unless_exists = yes
}

#移除可通过议案-标识
OCF_proposal_can_passed_del_sign = {
	set_temp_variable = {
		alert_id = token:alert_OCF_proposal_passed
	}
	del_IRIS_alert = yes
}

#启用联邦预算草案
OCF_activate_federal_budget_draft = {
	set_variable = { OCF_federal_budget_proposal = 1 }
	set_temp_variable = { alert_id = token:alert_OCF_federal_budget_proposal }
	add_IRIS_alert_unless_exists = yes
}

#关闭联邦预算草案
OCF_close_federal_budget_draft = {
	set_variable = { OCF_federal_budget_proposal = 0 }
	set_temp_variable = { alert_id = token:alert_OCF_federal_budget_proposal }
	del_IRIS_alert = yes
}

#开支
OCF_expenses_1_max = {
	custom_effect_tooltip = {
		localization_key = OCF_EXPENSES_1_MAX_TT
		EXP = "[?OCF_expenses_1_max_temp]"
	}
	add_to_variable = { highest_1_x_threshold = OCF_expenses_1_max_temp }
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { highest_1_x_threshold > 10 } }
		set_variable = { highest_1_x_threshold = 10 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { highest_1_x_threshold < 1 } }
		set_variable = { highest_1_x_threshold = 1 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { highest_1_x_threshold < minimum_1_x_threshold } }
		set_variable = { highest_1_x_threshold = minimum_1_x_threshold }
	}
}
OCF_expenses_1_min = {

		EXP = "[?OCF_expenses_1_min_temp]"

		set_variable = { minimum_1_x_threshold = 10 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { minimum_1_x_threshold < 1 } }
		set_variable = { minimum_1_x_threshold = 1 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { minimum_1_x_threshold > highest_1_x_threshold } }
		set_variable = { minimum_1_x_threshold = highest_1_x_threshold }
	}
}

	custom_effect_tooltip = {
		localization_key = OCF_EXPENSES_3_MAX_TT
		EXP = "[?OCF_expenses_3_max_temp]"
	}
	add_to_variable = { highest_3_x_threshold = OCF_expenses_3_max_temp }
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { highest_3_x_threshold > 10 } }
		set_variable = { highest_3_x_threshold = 10 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { highest_3_x_threshold < 1 } }
		set_variable = { highest_3_x_threshold = 1 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { highest_3_x_threshold < minimum_3_x_threshold } }
		set_variable = { highest_3_x_threshold = minimum_3_x_threshold }
	}
}

	#行政开支 4

	add_to_temp_variable = { sign_click_temp_1 = minimum_1_x_threshold }
	multiply_temp_variable = { sign_click_temp_1 = 0.3 }
	round_temp_variable = sign_click_temp_1
	add_to_temp_variable = { sign_click_temp_1 = 1 }

	subtract_from_temp_variable = { sign_click_temp_1 = 4 }
	if = {
		limit = { sign_click_temp_1 > 0 }
		set_temp_variable = { OCF_federal_budget_proposal_political_power_factor_temp = 0.06 }
		set_temp_variable = { OCF_federal_budget_proposal_drift_defence_factor_temp = 0.12 }

		set_temp_variable = { OCF_federal_budget_proposal_political_power_factor_temp = 0.12 }

	}
	multiply_temp_variable = { OCF_federal_budget_proposal_political_power_factor_temp = sign_click_temp_1 }
	multiply_temp_variable = { OCF_federal_budget_proposal_drift_defence_factor_temp = sign_click_temp_1 }

#载入预算案最低值进度
OCF_loading_minimum_budget_progress = {
	clear_array = OCF_federal_budget_proposal_gui_lists_1_array
	clear_array = OCF_federal_budget_proposal_gui_lists_2_array
	clear_array = OCF_federal_budget_proposal_gui_lists_3_array
	clear_array = OCF_federal_budget_proposal_gui_lists_4_array
	clear_array = OCF_federal_budget_proposal_gui_lists_5_array
	clear_array = OCF_federal_budget_proposal_gui_lists_1_array_nonnull
	clear_array = OCF_federal_budget_proposal_gui_lists_2_array_nonnull
	clear_array = OCF_federal_budget_proposal_gui_lists_3_array_nonnull
	clear_array = OCF_federal_budget_proposal_gui_lists_4_array_nonnull
	clear_array = OCF_federal_budget_proposal_gui_lists_5_array_nonnull


	#载入最低值-黄点
	for_loop_effect = {
		start = 0
		end = minimum_1_x_threshold
		add_to_array = { OCF_federal_budget_proposal_gui_lists_1_array = 1 }
	}
	for_each_loop = {
		array = OCF_federal_budget_proposal_gui_lists_1_array
		value = v
		add_to_array = { OCF_federal_budget_proposal_gui_lists_1_array_nonnull = v }
	}
	set_temp_variable = { spare_temp = 10 }
	subtract_from_temp_variable = { spare_temp = minimum_1_x_threshold }
	for_loop_effect = {
		start = 0
		end = spare_temp
		add_to_array = { OCF_federal_budget_proposal_gui_lists_1_array = 3 }
	}


	for_loop_effect = {
		start = 0
		end = minimum_2_x_threshold
		add_to_array = { OCF_federal_budget_proposal_gui_lists_2_array = 1 }
	}
	for_each_loop = {
		array = OCF_federal_budget_proposal_gui_lists_2_array
		value = v
		add_to_array = { OCF_federal_budget_proposal_gui_lists_2_array_nonnull = v }
	}
	set_temp_variable = { spare_temp = 10 }
	subtract_from_temp_variable = { spare_temp = minimum_2_x_threshold }
	for_loop_effect = {
		start = 0
		end = spare_temp
		add_to_array = { OCF_federal_budget_proposal_gui_lists_2_array = 3 }
	}


	for_loop_effect = {
		start = 0
		end = minimum_3_x_threshold
		add_to_array = { OCF_federal_budget_proposal_gui_lists_3_array = 1 }
	}
	for_each_loop = {
		array = OCF_federal_budget_proposal_gui_lists_3_array
		value = v
		add_to_array = { OCF_federal_budget_proposal_gui_lists_3_array_nonnull = v }
	}
	set_temp_variable = { spare_temp = 10 }
	subtract_from_temp_variable = { spare_temp = minimum_3_x_threshold }
	for_loop_effect = {
		start = 0
		end = spare_temp
		add_to_array = { OCF_federal_budget_proposal_gui_lists_3_array = 3 }
	}


	for_loop_effect = {
		start = 0
		end = minimum_4_x_threshold
		add_to_array = { OCF_federal_budget_proposal_gui_lists_4_array = 1 }
	}
	for_each_loop = {
		array = OCF_federal_budget_proposal_gui_lists_4_array
		value = v
		add_to_array = { OCF_federal_budget_proposal_gui_lists_4_array_nonnull = v }
	}
	set_temp_variable = { spare_temp = 10 }
	subtract_from_temp_variable = { spare_temp = minimum_4_x_threshold }
	for_loop_effect = {
		start = 0
		end = spare_temp
		add_to_array = { OCF_federal_budget_proposal_gui_lists_4_array = 3 }
	}
	# log = "社会开支最小值为：[?minimum_4_x_threshold]"
	# log = "新增[?spare_temp]个空位"


	for_loop_effect = {
		start = 0
		end = minimum_5_x_threshold
		add_to_array = { OCF_federal_budget_proposal_gui_lists_5_array = 1 }
	}
	for_each_loop = {
		array = OCF_federal_budget_proposal_gui_lists_5_array
		value = v
		add_to_array = { OCF_federal_budget_proposal_gui_lists_5_array_nonnull = v }
	}
	set_temp_variable = { spare_temp = 10 }
	subtract_from_temp_variable = { spare_temp = minimum_5_x_threshold }
	for_loop_effect = {
		start = 0
		end = spare_temp
		add_to_array = { OCF_federal_budget_proposal_gui_lists_5_array = 3 }
	}
}

				}
			}
			OCF_dail_party^2 = {

					OCF_dail_party^2 = -1
				}
			}
			OCF_dail_party^3 = {
				add_to_variable = {
					OCF_dail_party^3 = -1
				}
			}
			OCF_dail_party^4 = {
				add_to_variable = {
					OCF_dail_party^4 = -1
				}
			}
			OCF_dail_party^5 = {
				add_to_variable = {
					OCF_dail_party^5 = -1
				}
			}
			OCF_dail_party^6 = {
				add_to_variable = {
					OCF_dail_party^6 = -1
				}
			}
			OCF_dail_party^7 = {
				add_to_variable = {
					OCF_dail_party^7 = -1
				}
			}
			OCF_dail_party^8 = {

					OCF_dail_party^8 = -1
				}
			}
		}
	}

#裁员到600
OCF_Layoffs_automatic = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				OCF_gridbox_seat_array_6 > 600
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = {
			OCF_Layoffs_automatic = OCF_gridbox_seat_array_6
		}
		add_to_temp_variable = {
			OCF_Layoffs_automatic = -600
		}
		for_loop_effect = {
			end = OCF_Layoffs_automatic
			OCF_Layoffs = yes
		}
	}
}

	custom_effect_tooltip = OCF_randomly_add_member_parliament_3_tt
	hidden_effect = {
		OCF_randomly_add_member_parliament_2 = yes
		OCF_randomly_add_member_parliament_1 = yes
	}
}

#计算政府影响力
OCF_calculate_government_influence = {
	if = {
		#大洋社会主义同盟
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = OCF_control_government_flag_1
		}
		set_variable = {
			OCF_gridbox_seat_array_original_relationship_variable_1 = 8
		}
		set_variable = {
			OCF_calculate_government_influence_variable = OCF_dail_party^1
		}
	}
	if = {
		#大洋联邦社会联盟党
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = OCF_control_government_flag_2
		}
		set_variable = {
			OCF_gridbox_seat_array_original_relationship_variable_2 = 8
		}
		set_variable = {
			OCF_calculate_government_influence_variable = OCF_dail_party^2
		}
	}
	if = {
		#改组派民主保全会
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = OCF_control_government_flag_3
		}
		set_variable = {
			OCF_gridbox_seat_array_original_relationship_variable_3 = 8
		}
		set_variable = {
			OCF_calculate_government_influence_variable = OCF_dail_party^3
		}
	}
	if = {
		#大洋联邦同盟党
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = OCF_control_government_flag_4
		}
		set_variable = {
			OCF_gridbox_seat_array_original_relationship_variable_4 = 8
		}
		set_variable = {
			OCF_calculate_government_influence_variable = OCF_dail_party^4
		}
	}
	if = {
		#党外人士
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = OCF_control_government_flag_5
		}
		set_variable = {
			OCF_gridbox_seat_array_original_relationship_variable_5 = 8
		}
		set_variable = {
			OCF_calculate_government_influence_variable = OCF_dail_party^5
		}
	}
	if = {
		#民族党
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = OCF_control_government_flag_6
		}
		set_variable = {
			OCF_gridbox_seat_array_original_relationship_variable_6 = 8
		}
		set_variable = {
			OCF_calculate_government_influence_variable = OCF_dail_party^6
		}
	}
	if = {
		#自由党
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = OCF_control_government_flag_7
		}
		set_variable = {
			OCF_gridbox_seat_array_original_relationship_variable_7 = 8
		}
		set_variable = {
			OCF_calculate_government_influence_variable = OCF_dail_party^7
		}
	}
	if = {
		#玛娜维护协会
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = OCF_control_government_flag_8
		}
		set_variable = {
			OCF_gridbox_seat_array_original_relationship_variable_8 = 8
		}
		set_variable = {
			OCF_calculate_government_influence_variable = OCF_dail_party^8
		}
	}
	#友好党派
	if = {
		#大洋社会主义同盟
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = OCF_control_government_flag_1_yes
		}
		set_variable = {
			OCF_gridbox_seat_array_original_relationship_variable_1 = 8
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			OCF_calculate_government_influence_variable = OCF_dail_party^1
		}
	}
	if = {
		#大洋联邦社会联盟党
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = OCF_control_government_flag_2_yes
		}
		set_variable = {
			OCF_gridbox_seat_array_original_relationship_variable_2 = 8
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			OCF_calculate_government_influence_variable = OCF_dail_party^2
		}
	}
	if = {
		#改组派民主保全会
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = OCF_control_government_flag_3_yes
		}
		set_variable = {
			OCF_gridbox_seat_array_original_relationship_variable_3 = 8
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			OCF_calculate_government_influence_variable = OCF_dail_party^3
		}
	}
	if = {
		#大洋联邦同盟党
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = OCF_control_government_flag_4_yes
		}
		set_variable = {
			OCF_gridbox_seat_array_original_relationship_variable_4 = 8
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			OCF_calculate_government_influence_variable = OCF_dail_party^4
		}
	}
	if = {
		#党外人士
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = OCF_control_government_flag_5_yes
		}
		set_variable = {
			OCF_gridbox_seat_array_original_relationship_variable_5 = 8
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			OCF_calculate_government_influence_variable = OCF_dail_party^5
		}
	}
	if = {
		#民族党
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = OCF_control_government_flag_6_yes
		}
		set_variable = {
			OCF_gridbox_seat_array_original_relationship_variable_6 = 8
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			OCF_calculate_government_influence_variable = OCF_dail_party^6
		}
	}
	if = {
		#自由党
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = OCF_control_government_flag_7_yes
		}
		set_variable = {
			OCF_gridbox_seat_array_original_relationship_variable_7 = 8
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			OCF_calculate_government_influence_variable = OCF_dail_party^7
		}
	}
	if = {
		#玛娜维护协会
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = OCF_control_government_flag_8_yes
		}
		set_variable = {
			OCF_gridbox_seat_array_original_relationship_variable_8 = 8
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			OCF_calculate_government_influence_variable = OCF_dail_party^8
		}
	}
	set_variable = {
		OCF_calculate_government_influence_variable_100 = OCF_calculate_government_influence_variable
	}
	divide_variable = {
		OCF_calculate_government_influence_variable_100 = OCF_gridbox_seat_array_6
	}
	OCF_Prevent_spillage = yes
}

#政府权威性
OCF_government_authority = {
	set_variable = {
		OCF_government_authority_variable = OCF_gridbox_seat_array_original_relationship_variable_1
	}
	add_to_variable = {
		OCF_government_authority_variable = OCF_gridbox_seat_array_original_relationship_variable_2
	}
	add_to_variable = {
		OCF_government_authority_variable = OCF_gridbox_seat_array_original_relationship_variable_3
	}
	add_to_variable = {
		OCF_government_authority_variable = OCF_gridbox_seat_array_original_relationship_variable_4
	}
	add_to_variable = {
		OCF_government_authority_variable = OCF_gridbox_seat_array_original_relationship_variable_5
	}
	add_to_variable = {
		OCF_government_authority_variable = OCF_gridbox_seat_array_original_relationship_variable_6
	}
	add_to_variable = {
		OCF_government_authority_variable = OCF_gridbox_seat_array_original_relationship_variable_7
	}
	add_to_variable = {
		OCF_government_authority_variable = OCF_gridbox_seat_array_original_relationship_variable_8
	}
	# divide_variable = {
	# 	OCF_government_authority_variable = 0.64
	# }
	divide_variable = {
		OCF_government_authority_variable = 0.6 #降低难度变为0.5
	}

	set_temp_variable = { ocf_authority_factor_temp = 1 }
	add_to_temp_variable = { ocf_authority_factor_temp = modifier@ocf_authority_factor }
	multiply_variable = { OCF_government_authority_variable = ocf_authority_factor_temp }
	add_to_variable = { OCF_government_authority_variable = modifier@ocf_authority }

	multiply_variable = {
		OCF_government_authority_variable = OCF_stability_variable_30
	}
	set_variable = {
		OCF_federal_government_max_planning_100 = OCF_government_authority_variable
	}
	multiply_variable = {
		OCF_federal_government_max_planning_100 = 0.12
	}
	set_variable = {
		OCF_federal_government_max_planning = OCF_federal_government_max_planning_100
	}
	multiply_variable = {
		OCF_federal_government_max_planning = 0.01
	}
	set_variable = {
		OCF_federal_government_planning_speed_100 = OCF_government_authority_variable
	}
	multiply_variable = {
		OCF_federal_government_planning_speed_100 = 0.18
	}
	set_variable = {
		OCF_federal_government_planning_speed = OCF_federal_government_planning_speed_100
	}
	multiply_variable = {
		OCF_federal_government_planning_speed = 0.01
	}
	set_variable = {
		OCF_federal_government_mobilization_speed_100 = OCF_government_authority_variable
	}
	multiply_variable = {
		OCF_federal_government_mobilization_speed_100 = 0.08
	}
	set_variable = {
		OCF_federal_government_mobilization_speed = OCF_federal_government_mobilization_speed_100
	}
	multiply_variable = {
		OCF_federal_government_mobilization_speed = 0.01
	}
	set_variable = {
		OCF_federal_government_political_power_factor_100 = OCF_government_authority_variable
	}
	multiply_variable = {
		OCF_federal_government_political_power_factor_100 = 0.3
	}
	set_variable = {
		OCF_federal_government_political_power_factor = OCF_federal_government_political_power_factor_100
	}
	multiply_variable = {
		OCF_federal_government_political_power_factor = 0.01
	}



	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { OCF_government_authority_variable < 0 } }
		set_variable = { OCF_government_authority_variable = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { OCF_government_authority_variable > 100 } }
		set_variable = { OCF_government_authority_variable = 100 }
	}
}

##     ## ######## ##       ##     ## ########  ######  ##     ##    ##     ## ########  ######   ####  #######  ##    ## ##     ## ########     ######   #######  ##        ##         #######  ##     ##    ##       ##     ## ##     ##    ##    ########
#输入变量 pie_chart_angle 角度
#输出变量 coordinate_x x坐标
OCF_calculation_x_position = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				pie_chart_angle > 180
			}
		}
		subtract_from_temp_variable = {
			pie_chart_angle = 180
		}
		set_temp_variable = {
			decreased = 1
		}
	}
	set_temp_variable = {
		up_s = pie_chart_angle
	}
	multiply_temp_variable = {
		up_s = 7
	}
	set_temp_variable = {
		up_s_2 = 180
	}
	subtract_from_temp_variable = {
		up_s_2 = pie_chart_angle
	}
	multiply_temp_variable = {
		up_s = up_s_2
	}
	set_temp_variable = {
		down_s = 50000
	}
	set_temp_variable = {
		down_s_2 = 180
	}
	subtract_from_temp_variable = {
		down_s_2 = pie_chart_angle
	}
	multiply_temp_variable = {
		down_s_2 = pie_chart_angle
	}
	subtract_from_temp_variable = {
		down_s = down_s_2
	}
	set_temp_variable = {
		coordinate_x = up_s
	}
	divide_temp_variable = {
		coordinate_x = down_s
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				decreased = 1
			}
		}
		multiply_temp_variable = {
			coordinate_x = -1
		}
		add_to_temp_variable = {
			pie_chart_angle = 180
		}
		set_temp_variable = {
			decreased = 0
		}
	}
}

#输入变量 pie_chart_angle 角度
#输出变量 coordinate_y y坐标
OCF_calculation_y_position = {
	set_temp_variable = {
		angle_init = pie_chart_angle
	}
	add_to_temp_variable = {
		pie_chart_angle = 90
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				pie_chart_angle > 180
			}
		}
		subtract_from_temp_variable = {
			pie_chart_angle = 180
		}
		set_temp_variable = {
			decreased = 1
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				pie_chart_angle > 180
			}
		}
		subtract_from_temp_variable = {
			pie_chart_angle = 180
		}
		set_temp_variable = {
			decreased = 0
		}
	}
	set_temp_variable = {
		up_s = pie_chart_angle
	}
	multiply_temp_variable = {
		up_s = 7
	}
	set_temp_variable = {
		up_s_2 = 180
	}
	subtract_from_temp_variable = {
		up_s_2 = pie_chart_angle
	}
	multiply_temp_variable = {
		up_s = up_s_2
	}
	set_temp_variable = {
		down_s = 50000
	}
	set_temp_variable = {
		down_s_2 = 180
	}
	subtract_from_temp_variable = {
		down_s_2 = pie_chart_angle
	}
	multiply_temp_variable = {
		down_s_2 = pie_chart_angle
	}
	subtract_from_temp_variable = {
		down_s = down_s_2
	}
	set_temp_variable = {
		coordinate_y = up_s
	}
	divide_temp_variable = {
		coordinate_y = down_s
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				decreased = 1
			}
		}
		multiply_temp_variable = {
			coordinate_y = -1
		}
		set_temp_variable = {
			decreased = 0
		}
	}
	set_temp_variable = {
		pie_chart_angle = angle_init
	}
}

#饼图百分比坐标刷新
OCF_refresh_pie_chart_percentage_coordinates = {
	set_temp_variable = {
		pie_chart_angle = factions_region^1
	}
	multiply_temp_variable = {
		pie_chart_angle = 3.4
	}
	OCF_calculation_x_position = yes
	multiply_temp_variable = {
		coordinate_x = 30
	}
	set_variable = {
		coordinate_x^1 = coordinate_x
	}
	OCF_calculation_y_position = yes
	multiply_temp_variable = {
		coordinate_y = -30
	}
	add_to_temp_variable = {
		coordinate_y = 60
	}
	set_variable = {
		coordinate_y^1 = coordinate_y
	}
	set_temp_variable = {
		pie_chart_angle = factions_region^2
	}
	multiply_temp_variable = {
		pie_chart_angle = 3.4
	}

#刷新全国支持率
OCF_tax_revenue_civil_factories_correctionresh_national_support_rate = {
	OCF = {
		OCF_calculate_winning_usage = yes
	}
	set_variable = {
		OCF.OCF_national_support_1 = 0
	}
	set_variable = {
		OCF.OCF_national_support_2 = 0
	}
	set_variable = {
		OCF.OCF_national_support_3 = 0
	}
	set_variable = {
		OCF.OCF_national_support_4 = 0
	}
	set_variable = {
		OCF.OCF_national_support_5 = 0
	}
	set_variable = {
		OCF.OCF_national_support_6 = 0
	}
	set_variable = {
		OCF.OCF_national_support_7 = 0
	}
	set_variable = {
		OCF.OCF_national_support_8 = 0
	}
	every_state = {
		limit = {
			OCF_votable_areas_triggers = yes
		}
		OCF = {
			add_to_variable = {
				OCF_national_support_1 = PREV.OCF_regional_support_rate^1
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				OCF_national_support_2 = PREV.OCF_regional_support_rate^2
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				OCF_national_support_3 = PREV.OCF_regional_support_rate^3
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				OCF_national_support_4 = PREV.OCF_regional_support_rate^4
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				OCF_national_support_5 = PREV.OCF_regional_support_rate^5
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				OCF_national_support_6 = PREV.OCF_regional_support_rate^6
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				OCF_national_support_7 = PREV.OCF_regional_support_rate^7
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				OCF_national_support_8 = PREV.OCF_regional_support_rate^8
			}
		}
	}
	set_variable = {
		OCF_national_support_all = OCF.OCF_national_support_1
	}
	add_to_variable = {
		OCF_national_support_all = OCF.OCF_national_support_2
	}
	add_to_variable = {
		OCF_national_support_all = OCF.OCF_national_support_3
	}
	add_to_variable = {
		OCF_national_support_all = OCF.OCF_national_support_4
	}
	add_to_variable = {
		OCF_national_support_all = OCF.OCF_national_support_5
	}
	add_to_variable = {
		OCF_national_support_all = OCF.OCF_national_support_6
	}
	add_to_variable = {
		OCF_national_support_all = OCF.OCF_national_support_7
	}
	add_to_variable = {
		OCF_national_support_all = OCF.OCF_national_support_8
	}
	multiply_variable = {
		OCF_national_support_all = 0.01
	}
	set_variable = {
		OCF_national_support_proportion^1 = OCF.OCF_national_support_1
	}
	set_variable = {
		OCF_national_support_proportion^2 = OCF.OCF_national_support_2
	}
	set_variable = {
		OCF_national_support_proportion^3 = OCF.OCF_national_support_3
	}
	set_variable = {
		OCF_national_support_proportion^4 = OCF.OCF_national_support_4
	}
	set_variable = {
		OCF_national_support_proportion^5 = OCF.OCF_national_support_5
	}
	set_variable = {
		OCF_national_support_proportion^6 = OCF.OCF_national_support_6
	}
	set_variable = {
		OCF_national_support_proportion^7 = OCF.OCF_national_support_7
	}
	set_variable = {
		OCF_national_support_proportion^8 = OCF.OCF_national_support_8
	}
	divide_variable = {
		OCF_national_support_proportion^1 = OCF_national_support_all
	}
	divide_variable = {
		OCF_national_support_proportion^2 = OCF_national_support_all
	}
	divide_variable = {
		OCF_national_support_proportion^3 = OCF_national_support_all

	}

#刷新地区支持率
OCF_refresh_regional_support_rate = {
	OCF = {
		OCF_calculate_winning_usage = yes
	}
	#读取该地区每个党派数量算总数
	set_variable = {
		THIS.regional_support_rate = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate^1
	}
	add_to_variable = {
		THIS.regional_support_rate = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate^2
	}
	add_to_variable = {
		THIS.regional_support_rate = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate^3
	}
	add_to_variable = {
		THIS.regional_support_rate = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate^4
	}
	add_to_variable = {
		THIS.regional_support_rate = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate^5
	}
	add_to_variable = {
		THIS.regional_support_rate = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate^6
	}
	add_to_variable = {
		THIS.regional_support_rate = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate^7
	}
	add_to_variable = {
		THIS.regional_support_rate = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate^8
	}
	#保留原数据
	set_variable = {
		THIS.regional_support_rate_100 = THIS.regional_support_rate
	}
	multiply_variable = {
		THIS.regional_support_rate_100 = 0.01
	}
	#计算占比
	set_variable = {
		THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_proportion^2 = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate^2
	}
	set_variable = {
		THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_proportion^1 = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_proportion^2
	}
	add_to_variable = {
		THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_proportion^1 = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate^1
	}
	set_variable = {
		THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_proportion^5 = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_proportion^1
	}
	add_to_variable = {
		THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_proportion^5 = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate^5
	}
	set_variable = {
		THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_proportion^3 = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_proportion^5
	}
	add_to_variable = {
		THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_proportion^3 = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate^3
	}
	set_variable = {
		THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_proportion^4 = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_proportion^3
	}
	add_to_variable = {
		THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_proportion^4 = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate^4
	}
	set_variable = {
		THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_proportion^7 = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_proportion^4
	}
	add_to_variable = {
		THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_proportion^7 = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate^7
	}
	set_variable = {
		THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_proportion^8 = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_proportion^7
	}
	add_to_variable = {
		THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_proportion^8 = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate^8
	}
	set_variable = {
		THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_proportion^6 = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_proportion^8
	}
	add_to_variable = {
		THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_proportion^6 = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate^6
	}
	divide_variable = {
		THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_proportion^1 = THIS.regional_support_rate_100
	}
	divide_variable = {
		THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_proportion^2 = THIS.regional_support_rate_100
	}
	divide_variable = {
		THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_proportion^3 = THIS.regional_support_rate_100
	}
	divide_variable = {
		THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_proportion^4 = THIS.regional_support_rate_100
	}
	divide_variable = {
		THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_proportion^5 = THIS.regional_support_rate_100
	}
	divide_variable = {
		THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_proportion^6 = THIS.regional_support_rate_100
	}
	divide_variable = {
		THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_proportion^7 = THIS.regional_support_rate_100
	}
	divide_variable = {
		THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_proportion^8 = THIS.regional_support_rate_100
	}
	set_variable = {
		THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_storage^1 = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate^1
	}
	set_variable = {
		THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_storage^2 = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate^2
	}
	set_variable = {
		THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_storage^3 = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate^3
	}
	set_variable = {
		THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_storage^4 = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate^4
	}
	set_variable = {
		THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_storage^5 = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate^5
	}
	set_variable = {
		THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_storage^6 = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate^6
	}
	set_variable = {
		THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_storage^7 = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate^7
	}
	set_variable = {
		THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_storage^8 = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate^8
	}
	divide_variable = {
		THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_storage^1 = THIS.regional_support_rate_100
	}
	divide_variable = {
		THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_storage^2 = THIS.regional_support_rate_100
	}
	divide_variable = {
		THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_storage^3 = THIS.regional_support_rate_100
	}
	divide_variable = {
		THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_storage^4 = THIS.regional_support_rate_100
	}
	divide_variable = {
		THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_storage^5 = THIS.regional_support_rate_100
	}
	divide_variable = {
		THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_storage^6 = THIS.regional_support_rate_100
	}
	divide_variable = {
		THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_storage^7 = THIS.regional_support_rate_100
	}
	divide_variable = {
		THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_storage^8 = THIS.regional_support_rate_100
	}
	#把数据传入后端， 显示饼图
	OCF = {
		set_variable = {
			factions_region^1 = PREV.OCF_regional_support_rate_proportion^1
		}
		set_variable = {
			factions_region^2 = PREV.OCF_regional_support_rate_proportion^2
		}
		set_variable = {
			factions_region^3 = PREV.OCF_regional_support_rate_proportion^3
		}
		set_variable = {
			factions_region^4 = PREV.OCF_regional_support_rate_proportion^4
		}
		set_variable = {
			factions_region^5 = PREV.OCF_regional_support_rate_proportion^5
		}
		set_variable = {
			factions_region^6 = PREV.OCF_regional_support_rate_proportion^6
		}
		set_variable = {
			factions_region^7 = PREV.OCF_regional_support_rate_proportion^7
		}
		set_variable = {
			factions_region^8 = PREV.OCF_regional_support_rate_proportion^8
		}
		#储存真实百分比
		set_variable = {
			THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_storage^1 = PREV.OCF_regional_support_rate_storage^1
		}
		set_variable = {
			THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_storage^2 = PREV.OCF_regional_support_rate_storage^2
		}
		set_variable = {
			THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_storage^3 = PREV.OCF_regional_support_rate_storage^3
		}
		set_variable = {
			THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_storage^4 = PREV.OCF_regional_support_rate_storage^4
		}
		set_variable = {
			THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_storage^5 = PREV.OCF_regional_support_rate_storage^5
		}
		set_variable = {
			THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_storage^6 = PREV.OCF_regional_support_rate_storage^6
		}
		set_variable = {
			THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_storage^7 = PREV.OCF_regional_support_rate_storage^7
		}
		set_variable = {
			THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate_storage^8 = PREV.OCF_regional_support_rate_storage^8
		}
	}
	#计算当前最高值和计算可能胜选党派
	set_variable = {
		THIS.regional_leaders = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate^1
	}
	set_variable = {
		THIS.regional_leaders_2 = 1
	}
	set_variable = {
		PREV.OCF_superior_victory_1 = 0
	}
	#初始化各个党派
	set_variable = {
		PREV.OCF_superior_victory_2 = 0
	}
	set_variable = {
		PREV.OCF_superior_victory_3 = 0
	}
	set_variable = {
		PREV.OCF_superior_victory_4 = 0
	}
	set_variable = {
		PREV.OCF_superior_victory_5 = 0
	}
	set_variable = {
		PREV.OCF_superior_victory_6 = 0
	}
	set_variable = {
		PREV.OCF_superior_victory_7 = 0
	}
	set_variable = {
		PREV.OCF_superior_victory_8 = 0
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				THIS.regional_leaders < THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate^2
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			THIS.regional_leaders = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate^2
		}
		set_variable = {
			THIS.regional_leaders_2 = 2
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			PREV.OCF_superior_victory_2 = 1
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				THIS.regional_leaders < THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate^3
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			THIS.regional_leaders = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate^3
		}
		set_variable = {
			THIS.regional_leaders_2 = 3
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			PREV.OCF_superior_victory_3 = 1
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				THIS.regional_leaders < THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate^4
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			THIS.regional_leaders = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate^4
		}
		set_variable = {
			THIS.regional_leaders_2 = 4
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			PREV.OCF_superior_victory_4 = 1
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				THIS.regional_leaders < THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate^5
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			THIS.regional_leaders = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate^5
		}
		set_variable = {
			THIS.regional_leaders_2 = 5
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			PREV.OCF_superior_victory_5 = 1
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				THIS.regional_leaders < THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate^6
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			THIS.regional_leaders = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate^6
		}
		set_variable = {
			THIS.regional_leaders_2 = 6
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			PREV.OCF_superior_victory_6 = 1
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				THIS.regional_leaders < THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate^7
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			THIS.regional_leaders = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate^7
		}
		set_variable = {
			THIS.regional_leaders_2 = 7
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			PREV.OCF_superior_victory_7 = 1
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				THIS.regional_leaders < THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate^8
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			THIS.regional_leaders = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate^8
		}
		set_variable = {
			THIS.regional_leaders_2 = 8
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			PREV.OCF_superior_victory_8 = 1
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				THIS.regional_leaders_2 = 1
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			PREV.OCF_superior_victory_1 = 1
		}
	}
	#计算可能胜出党派
	set_variable = {
		PREV.OCF_superior_victory_0 = 0
	}
	#胜选派
	set_variable = {
		PREV.OCF_superior_victory_max = 0
	}
	#最大胜选派
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				PREV.OCF_superior_victory_1 > PREV.OCF_superior_victory_max
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			PREV.OCF_superior_victory_0 = 1
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				PREV.OCF_superior_victory_2 > PREV.OCF_superior_victory_max
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			PREV.OCF_superior_victory_0 = 2
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				PREV.OCF_superior_victory_3 > PREV.OCF_superior_victory_max
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			PREV.OCF_superior_victory_0 = 3
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				PREV.OCF_superior_victory_4 > PREV.OCF_superior_victory_max
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			PREV.OCF_superior_victory_0 = 4
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				PREV.OCF_superior_victory_5 > PREV.OCF_superior_victory_max
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			PREV.OCF_superior_victory_0 = 5
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				PREV.OCF_superior_victory_6 > PREV.OCF_superior_victory_max
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			PREV.OCF_superior_victory_0 = 6
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				PREV.OCF_superior_victory_7 > PREV.OCF_superior_victory_max
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			PREV.OCF_superior_victory_0 = 7
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				PREV.OCF_superior_victory_8 > PREV.OCF_superior_victory_max
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			PREV.OCF_superior_victory_0 = 8
		}
	}
	OCF_government_authority = yes
	OCF = {
		OCF_refresh_pie_chart_percentage_coordinates = yes
	}
}

#刷新可能获胜党派(暂时废弃)
OCF_Refreshing_possible_winning_parties = {
	every_state = {
		limit = {
			OCF_votable_areas_triggers = yes
		}
	}
}

#临时大选代码
OCF_election_results = {
	OCF_calculate_winning_usage = yes
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = has_OCF_101_flag
		}
		country_event = {
			id = OCF.25
			days = 5
		}
	}
	else = {
		country_event = {
			id = OCF.101
			days = 1
		}
	}
}

#计算获胜使用
OCF_calculate_winning_usage = {
	set_variable = {
		OCF.OCF_election_results_1 = 0
	}
	set_variable = {
		OCF.OCF_election_results_2 = 0
	}
	set_variable = {
		OCF.OCF_election_results_3 = 0
	}
	set_variable = {
		OCF.OCF_election_results_4 = 0
	}
	set_variable = {
		OCF.OCF_election_results_5 = 0
	}
	set_variable = {
		OCF.OCF_election_results_6 = 0
	}
	set_variable = {
		OCF.OCF_election_results_7 = 0
	}
	set_variable = {
		OCF.OCF_election_results_8 = 0
	}
	every_state = {
		limit = {
			OCF_votable_areas_triggers = yes
		}
		set_variable = {
			OCF.OCF_election_results_state_MAX = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate^1
		}
		set_variable = {
			OCF.OCF_election_results_state_winning = 1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					OCF.OCF_election_results_state_MAX < THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate^2
				}
			}
			set_variable = {
				OCF.OCF_election_results_state_MAX = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate^2
			}
			set_variable = {
				OCF.OCF_election_results_state_winning = 2
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					OCF.OCF_election_results_state_MAX < THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate^3
				}
			}
			set_variable = {
				OCF.OCF_election_results_state_MAX = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate^3
			}
			set_variable = {
				OCF.OCF_election_results_state_winning = 3
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					OCF.OCF_election_results_state_MAX < THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate^4
				}
			}
			set_variable = {
				OCF.OCF_election_results_state_MAX = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate^4
			}
			set_variable = {
				OCF.OCF_election_results_state_winning = 4
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					OCF.OCF_election_results_state_MAX < THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate^5
				}
			}
			set_variable = {
				OCF.OCF_election_results_state_MAX = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate^5
			}
			set_variable = {
				OCF.OCF_election_results_state_winning = 5
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					OCF.OCF_election_results_state_MAX < THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate^6
				}
			}
			set_variable = {
				OCF.OCF_election_results_state_MAX = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate^6
			}
			set_variable = {
				OCF.OCF_election_results_state_winning = 6
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					OCF.OCF_election_results_state_MAX < THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate^7
				}
			}
			set_variable = {
				OCF.OCF_election_results_state_MAX = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate^7
			}
			set_variable = {
				OCF.OCF_election_results_state_winning = 7
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					OCF.OCF_election_results_state_MAX < THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate^8
				}
			}
			set_variable = {
				OCF.OCF_election_results_state_MAX = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate^8
			}
			set_variable = {
				OCF.OCF_election_results_state_winning = 8
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					OCF.OCF_election_results_state_winning = 1
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				OCF.OCF_election_results_1 = 1
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					OCF.OCF_election_results_state_winning = 2
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				OCF.OCF_election_results_2 = 1
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					OCF.OCF_election_results_state_winning = 3
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				OCF.OCF_election_results_3 = 1
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					OCF.OCF_election_results_state_winning = 4
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				OCF.OCF_election_results_4 = 1
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					OCF.OCF_election_results_state_winning = 5
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				OCF.OCF_election_results_5 = 1
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					OCF.OCF_election_results_state_winning = 6
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				OCF.OCF_election_results_6 = 1
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					OCF.OCF_election_results_state_winning = 7
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				OCF.OCF_election_results_7 = 1
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					OCF.OCF_election_results_state_winning = 8
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				OCF.OCF_election_results_8 = 1
			}
		}
	}
	set_variable = {
		OCF.OCF_election_results_max = OCF.OCF_election_results_1
	}
	set_variable = {
		OCF.OCF_election_results_winning = 1
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				OCF.OCF_election_results_2 > OCF.OCF_election_results_max
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			OCF.OCF_election_results_winning = 2
		}
		set_variable = {
			OCF.OCF_election_results_max = OCF.OCF_election_results_2
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				OCF.OCF_election_results_3 > OCF.OCF_election_results_max
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			OCF.OCF_election_results_winning = 3
		}
		set_variable = {
			OCF.OCF_election_results_max = OCF.OCF_election_results_3
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				OCF.OCF_election_results_4 > OCF.OCF_election_results_max
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			OCF.OCF_election_results_winning = 4
		}
		set_variable = {
			OCF.OCF_election_results_max = OCF.OCF_election_results_4
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				OCF.OCF_election_results_5 > OCF.OCF_election_results_max
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			OCF.OCF_election_results_winning = 5
		}
		set_variable = {
			OCF.OCF_election_results_max = OCF.OCF_election_results_5
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				OCF.OCF_election_results_6 > OCF.OCF_election_results_max
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			OCF.OCF_election_results_winning = 6
		}
		set_variable = {
			OCF.OCF_election_results_max = OCF.OCF_election_results_6
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				OCF.OCF_election_results_7 > OCF.OCF_election_results_max
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			OCF.OCF_election_results_winning = 7
		}
		set_variable = {
			OCF.OCF_election_results_max = OCF.OCF_election_results_7
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				OCF.OCF_election_results_8 > OCF.OCF_election_results_max
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			OCF.OCF_election_results_winning = 8
		}
		set_variable = {
			OCF.OCF_election_results_max = OCF.OCF_election_results_8
		}
	}
