#调整至100值
OCF_region_supports_formatting = {
	hidden_effect = {
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				OCF_computable_region_triggers = yes
			}
			set_temp_variable = {
				THIS.temp = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate^1
			}
			add_to_temp_variable = {
				THIS.temp = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate^2
			}
			add_to_temp_variable = {
				THIS.temp = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate^3
			}
			add_to_temp_variable = {
				THIS.temp = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate^4
			}
			add_to_temp_variable = {
				THIS.temp = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate^5
			}
			add_to_temp_variable = {
				THIS.temp = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate^6
			}
			add_to_temp_variable = {
				THIS.temp = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate^7
			}
			add_to_temp_variable = {
				THIS.temp = THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate^8
			}
			#如果超过100
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						THIS.temp > 100
					}
				}
				add_to_temp_variable = {
					THIS.temp = -100
				}
				for_loop_effect = {
					end = THIS.temp
					random_list = {
						THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate^1 = {
							add_to_variable = {
								THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate^1 = -1
							}
						}
						THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate^2 = {
							add_to_variable = {
								THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate^2 = -1
							}
						}
						THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate^3 = {
							add_to_variable = {
								THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate^3 = -1
							}
						}
						THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate^4 = {
							add_to_variable = {
								THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate^4 = -1
							}
						}
						THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate^5 = {
							add_to_variable = {
								THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate^5 = -1
							}
						}
						THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate^6 = {
							add_to_variable = {
								THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate^6 = -1
							}
						}
						THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate^7 = {
							add_to_variable = {
								THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate^7 = -1
							}
						}
						THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate^8 = {
							add_to_variable = {
								THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate^8 = -1
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			#如果小于100
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						THIS.temp < 100
					}
				}
				add_to_temp_variable = {
					THIS.temp = -100
				}
				multiply_temp_variable = {
					THIS.temp = -1
				}
				for_loop_effect = {
					end = THIS.temp
					random_list = {
						THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate^1 = {
							add_to_variable = {
								THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate^1 = 1
							}
						}
						THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate^2 = {
							add_to_variable = {
								THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate^2 = 1
							}
						}
						THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate^3 = {
							add_to_variable = {
								THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate^3 = 1
							}
						}
						THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate^4 = {
							add_to_variable = {
								THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate^4 = 1
							}
						}
						THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate^5 = {
							add_to_variable = {
								THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate^5 = 1
							}
						}
						THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate^6 = {
							add_to_variable = {
								THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate^6 = 1
							}
						}
						THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate^7 = {
							add_to_variable = {
								THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate^7 = 1
							}
						}
						THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate^8 = {
							add_to_variable = {
								THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate^8 = 1
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

#打压党派
OCF_suppress_political_parties = {
	OCF_refresh_regional_support_rate = yes
	OCF_Prevent_spillage = yes
	OCF = {
		OCF_government_authority = yes
		OCF_calculate_winning_usage = yes
		OCF_region_supports_formatting = yes
	}
}

OCF_suppress_political_parties_1 = {
	OCF_gridbox_seat_array_original_relationship_variable_1^del = yes
	custom_effect_tooltip = OCF_changes_party_relations
	custom_effect_tooltip = OCF_reduce_relationships_I_3
	every_state = {
		limit = {
			state = ROOT.OCF_select_region_variable
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = OCF_Party_TT_6_2_1_tt
		add_to_variable = {
			THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate^1 = -35
		}
		add_to_array = {
			global.OCF_changes_in_parliamentary_history_change_record_array = 25
			index = 0
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate^1 < 0
				}
			}
			set_variable = {
				THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate^1 = 0
			}
		}
		OCF_changes_in_parliamentary_history_list_dates_add = yes
		OCF_suppress_political_parties = yes
	}
}

OCF_supporting_political_parties_3 = {
	OCF_gridbox_seat_array_original_relationship_variable_3^add = yes
	custom_effect_tooltip = OCF_changes_party_relations
	custom_effect_tooltip = OCF_reduce_relationships_III_8
	every_state = {
		limit = {
			state = ROOT.OCF_select_region_variable
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = OCF_Party_TT_5_2_3_tt
		add_to_variable = {
			THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate^3 = 20
		}
		add_to_array = {
			global.OCF_changes_in_parliamentary_history_change_record_array = 19
			index = 0
		}
		OCF_changes_in_parliamentary_history_list_dates_add = yes
		OCF_supporting_political_parties = yes
	}

#增加党派地区支持度
#接受临时变量
#factions_temp 派系
#seat_temp 席位
#弃用代码
OCF_increase_support_for_political_parties_regions = {
	meta_effect = {
		text = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						seat_temp < 0
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = {
							seat_temp > -15
						}
					}
					set_temp_variable = {
						temp_icon = token:OCF_reduced_effectiveness_1
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = {
							seat_temp > -30
						}
					}
					set_temp_variable = {
						temp_icon = token:OCF_reduced_effectiveness_2
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = {
							seat_temp > -45
						}
					}
					set_temp_variable = {
						temp_icon = token:OCF_reduced_effectiveness_3
					}
				}
				else = {
					set_temp_variable = {
						temp_icon = token:OCF_reduced_effectiveness_4
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = {
							seat_temp < 10
						}
					}
					set_temp_variable = {
						temp_icon = token:OCF_effect_lifting_0
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = {
							seat_temp < 25
						}
					}
					set_temp_variable = {
						temp_icon = token:OCF_effect_lifting_1
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = {
							seat_temp < 40
						}
					}
					set_temp_variable = {
						temp_icon = token:OCF_effect_lifting_2
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = {
							seat_temp < 55
						}
					}
					set_temp_variable = {
						temp_icon = token:OCF_effect_lifting_3
					}
				}
				else = {
					set_temp_variable = {
						temp_icon = token:OCF_effect_lifting_4
					}
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = {
				localization_key = OCF_increase_support_for_political_parties_regions_tt
				INDENTATION = ""
				ICON = "[?temp_icon.GetTokenLocalizedKey]"
				FACTIONS = "OCF_parliamentary_parties_1"
				SUPPORT = "[?OCF.OCF_national_support_[FACTIONS]_proportion|2]"
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate^[FACTIONS] = [SEAT]
			}
		}
		SEAT = "[?seat_temp]"		#席位
		FACTIONS = "[?factions_temp]"		#派系编号
	}
}

#将增加随机派系支持
OCF_random_region_supports_changes_add = {
	custom_effect_tooltip = OCF_random_region_supports_changes_add_tt
	hidden_effect = {
		random_list = {
			1 = {
				add_to_variable = {
					THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate^1 = 20
				}
			}
			1 = {
				add_to_variable = {
					THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate^2 = 20
				}
			}
			1 = {
				add_to_variable = {
					THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate^3 = 20
				}
			}
			1 = {
				add_to_variable = {
					THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate^4 = 20
				}
			}
			1 = {
				add_to_variable = {
					THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate^5 = 20
				}
			}
			1 = {
				add_to_variable = {
					THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate^6 = 20
				}
			}
			1 = {
				add_to_variable = {
					THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate^7 = 20
				}
			}
			1 = {
				add_to_variable = {
					THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate^8 = 20
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

#将减少随机派系支持
OCF_random_region_supports_changes_del = {
	custom_effect_tooltip = OCF_random_region_supports_changes_del_tt
	hidden_effect = {
		random_list = {
			1 = {
				add_to_variable = {
					THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate^1 = -20
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = {
							THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate^1 < 0
						}
					}
					set_variable = {
						THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate^1 = 0
					}
				}
			}
			1 = {
				add_to_variable = {
					THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate^2 = -20
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = {
							THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate^2 < 0
						}
					}
					set_variable = {
						THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate^2 = 0
					}
				}
			}
			1 = {
				add_to_variable = {
					THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate^3 = -20
				}

					limit = {
						check_variable = {

					limit = {

						}

						}
					}
					set_variable = {
						THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate^7 = 0
					}
				}

					THIS.OCF_regional_support_rate^8 = -20

					limit = {

#刷新所有地区数据
OCF_refresh_all_regional_data = {
	every_state = {
		limit = {
			OCF_computable_region_triggers = yes
		}
		OCF_refresh_regional_support_rate = yes
	}
	OCF_region_supports_formatting = yes
}

#切换党魁
OCF_switching_party_leaders = {
	OCF = {
		set_variable = {
			OCF_party_opened_tab = 1
		}
		#将界面退出
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					OCF.OCF_show_all_party_leaders = 5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						OCF_Party_SubGUI_2_lists_v = token:OCF_Izumi_Sojiro
					}
				}
				add_ideas = OCF_idea_Izumi_Sojiro
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						OCF_Party_SubGUI_2_lists_v = token:OCF_Hiiragi_Tsukasa
					}
				}
				add_ideas = OCF_idea_Hiiragi_Tsukasa
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						OCF_Party_SubGUI_2_lists_v = token:OCF_Kuroi_Nanako
					}
				}
				add_ideas = OCF_idea_Kuroi_Nanako
			}
			set_variable = {
				OCF_party_leader^5 = OCF_Party_SubGUI_2_lists_v
			}
			#定义显示谁
		}
	}
}

#刷新党魁
OCF_refresh_party_leader = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = OCF_control_government_flag_1
			NOT = {
				has_idea = OCF_Labor_Conference
			}
		}
		add_ideas = OCF_Labor_Conference
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = OCF_control_government_flag_2
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = OCF_control_government_flag_3
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = OCF_control_government_flag_4
			NOT = {
				has_idea = OCF_idea_Shiina_Mayuri
			}
		}
		add_ideas = OCF_idea_Shiina_Mayuri
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = OCF_control_government_flag_5
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					OCF_party_leader^5 = token:OCF_Izumi_Sojiro
				}
			}
			add_ideas = OCF_idea_Izumi_Sojiro
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					OCF_party_leader^5 = token:OCF_Hiiragi_Tsukasa
				}
			}
			add_ideas = OCF_idea_Hiiragi_Tsukasa
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					OCF_party_leader^5 = token:OCF_Kuroi_Nanako
				}
			}
			add_ideas = OCF_idea_Kuroi_Nanako
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = OCF_control_government_flag_6
			NOT = {
				has_idea = OCF_idea_Altair
			}
		}
		add_ideas = OCF_idea_Altair
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = OCF_control_government_flag_7
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = OCF_control_government_flag_8
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = OCF_control_government_flag_1_yes
			NOT = {
				has_idea = OCF_Labor_Conference
			}
		}
		add_ideas = OCF_Labor_Conference
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = OCF_control_government_flag_2_yes
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = OCF_control_government_flag_3_yes
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = OCF_control_government_flag_4_yes
			NOT = {
				has_idea = OCF_idea_Shiina_Mayuri
			}
		}
		add_ideas = OCF_idea_Shiina_Mayuri
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = OCF_control_government_flag_5_yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					OCF_party_leader^5 = token:OCF_Izumi_Sojiro
				}
			}
			add_ideas = OCF_idea_Izumi_Sojiro
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					OCF_party_leader^5 = token:OCF_Hiiragi_Tsukasa
				}
			}
			add_ideas = OCF_idea_Hiiragi_Tsukasa
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					OCF_party_leader^5 = token:OCF_Kuroi_Nanako
				}
			}
			add_ideas = OCF_idea_Kuroi_Nanako
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = OCF_control_government_flag_6_yes
			NOT = {
				has_idea = OCF_idea_Altair
			}
		}
		add_ideas = OCF_idea_Altair
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = OCF_control_government_flag_7_yes
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = OCF_control_government_flag_8_yes
		}
	}
}

#清除当前执政党-结盟
OCF_eliminate_current_ruling_party = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = OCF_control_government_flag_1
		}
		clr_country_flag = OCF_control_government_flag_1
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = OCF_control_government_flag_2

#清除所有副领导人 现在这个没必要了，我精神加了自动移除
OCF_clear_all_deputy_leaders = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = OCF_idea_parliament
		}
		remove_ideas = OCF_idea_parliament
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = OCF_idea_Hiiragi_Kagami
		}
		remove_ideas = OCF_idea_Hiiragi_Kagami
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = INP_idea_Reed_The_Flame_Shadow
		}
		remove_ideas = INP_idea_Reed_The_Flame_Shadow
	}
}

#选举后重置执政党
OCF_reset_ruling_party = {
	OCF_eliminate_current_ruling_party = yes
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				OCF.OCF_election_results_winning = 1
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = OCF_control_government_flag_1
		OCF_elected_faction_1 = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				OCF.OCF_election_results_winning = 2
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = OCF_control_government_flag_2
		OCF_elected_faction_2 = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				OCF.OCF_election_results_winning = 3
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = OCF_control_government_flag_3
		OCF_elected_faction_3 = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				OCF.OCF_election_results_winning = 4
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = OCF_control_government_flag_4
		OCF_elected_faction_4 = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				OCF.OCF_election_results_winning = 5
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = OCF_control_government_flag_5
		OCF_elected_faction_5 = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				OCF.OCF_election_results_winning = 6
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = OCF_control_government_flag_6
		OCF_elected_faction_6 = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				OCF.OCF_election_results_winning = 7
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = OCF_control_government_flag_7
		OCF_elected_faction_7 = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				OCF.OCF_election_results_winning = 8
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = OCF_control_government_flag_8
		OCF_elected_faction_8 = yes
	}
	OCF_party_relations_refresh = yes
}

		long_name = OCF_parties_1_long
		name = OCF_parties_1
	}

#启动弹劾系统
OCF_activate_impeachment_system = {
	set_variable = {
		OCF.impeach_supporters = 0
	}
	#参议院弹劾支持者
	set_variable = {
		OCF.impeach_supporters_senate_1 = 0
	}
	set_variable = {
		OCF.impeach_supporters_senate_2 = 0
	}
	set_variable = {
		OCF.impeach_supporters_senate_3 = 0
	}
	set_variable = {
		OCF.impeach_supporters_senate_4 = 0
	}
	set_variable = {
		OCF.impeach_supporters_senate_5 = 0
	}
	set_variable = {
		OCF.impeach_supporters_senate_6 = 0
	}
	set_variable = {
		OCF.impeach_supporters_senate_7 = 0
	}
	set_variable = {
		OCF.impeach_supporters_senate_8 = 0
	}
	set_variable = {
		OCF.impeach_supporters_senate = 0
	}
	#众议院弹劾支持者 总和
}

#计算众议院弹劾人数
OCF_calculate_number_impeached_members_house_representatives = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			OCF_in_government_factions_1 = yes
		}
		set_variable = {
			OCF.impeach_supporters_senate_1 = 0
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			OCF_in_government_factions_2 = yes
		}
		set_variable = {
			OCF.impeach_supporters_senate_2 = 0
		}
	}
	if = {

OCF_regarding_federal_parliament_add = {
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { GetOcfParliamentaryIntroductionWindowTitleDesc_var > 9 } }
		set_variable = { GetOcfParliamentaryIntroductionWindowTitleDesc_var = 1 }
	}
	else = {
		add_to_variable = { GetOcfParliamentaryIntroductionWindowTitleDesc_var = 1 }
		OCF_regarding_federal_parliament_operate = yes
	}
}
OCF_regarding_federal_parliament_del = {
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { GetOcfParliamentaryIntroductionWindowTitleDesc_var < 2 } }
		set_variable = { GetOcfParliamentaryIntroductionWindowTitleDesc_var = 10 }
	}
	else = {
		add_to_variable = { GetOcfParliamentaryIntroductionWindowTitleDesc_var = -1 }
		OCF_regarding_federal_parliament_operate = yes
	}
}

OCF_regarding_federal_parliament_operate = {
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { GetOcfParliamentaryIntroductionWindowTitleDesc_var = 5 } }
		set_country_flag = OCF_entering_parliament_flag
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { GetOcfParliamentaryIntroductionWindowTitleDesc_var > 5 }
			check_variable = { GetOcfParliamentaryIntroductionWindowTitleDesc_var < 8 }
		}
		set_variable = { OCF_party_opened_tab = 1 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { GetOcfParliamentaryIntroductionWindowTitleDesc_var = 8 } }
		set_country_flag = OCF_entering_parliament_flag
		set_variable = { OCF_party_opened_tab = 2 }
		OCF_show_all_party_leaders_5 = yes
	}
}





OCF_strengthening_artificial_intelligence = {
	hidden_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_ai = yes
				controls_state = 826
				controls_state = 115
				controls_state = 841
				controls_state = 842
				controls_state = 843
				controls_state = 844
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = OCF_control_government_flag_8 } OCF_mana_staffing_refresh = yes
			}
			else = { OCF_tank_staffing_refresh = yes }
			OCF_artificial_intelligence_flashing_in = yes
			OCF_artificial_intelligence_removal = yes
			OCF_infantry_staffing_refresh = yes
			OCF_artificial_intelligence_flashing_in = yes
			OCF_artificial_intelligence_removal = yes
		}
	}
}
